#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Prior art scan — runs on idea-new / idea-pivot issues.

Searches GitHub repos and HN discussions for existing solutions,
then posts a summary comment on the issue.
"""

import json
import os
import sys
import time
from urllib.parse import quote_plus

import httpx

GITHUB_TOKEN = os.environ["GITHUB_TOKEN"]
ISSUE_TITLE = os.environ["ISSUE_TITLE"]
ISSUE_NUMBER = os.environ["ISSUE_NUMBER"]
REPO = os.environ["REPO"]
ISSUE_BODY = os.environ.get("ISSUE_BODY", "")

GITHUB_API = "https://api.github.com"
HN_API = "https://hn.algolia.com/api/v1"

HEADERS = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {GITHUB_TOKEN}",
    "Accept": "application/vnd.github+json",
    "X-GitHub-Api-Version": "2022-11-28",
}


def search_github_repos(query: str, max_results: int = 10) -> list[dict]:
    """Search GitHub for repositories matching the query."""
    url = f"{GITHUB_API}/search/repositories"
    params = {
        "q": query,
        "sort": "stars",
        "order": "desc",
        "per_page": max_results,
    }
    try:
        resp = httpx.get(url, headers=HEADERS, params=params, timeout=15)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        data = resp.json()
        return [
            {
                "name": r["full_name"],
                "stars": r["stargazers_count"],
                "description": (r.get("description") or "")[:120],
                "url": r["html_url"],
                "updated": r["updated_at"][:10],
                "language": r.get("language") or "—",
            }
            for r in data.get("items", [])[:max_results]
        ]
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"GitHub search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        return []


def search_hn(query: str, max_results: int = 5) -> list[dict]:
    """Search Hacker News for discussions matching the query."""
    url = f"{HN_API}/search"
    params = {
        "query": query,
        "tags": "story",
        "hitsPerPage": max_results,
        "numericFilters": "points>5",
    }
    try:
        resp = httpx.get(url, params=params, timeout=15)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        data = resp.json()
        return [
            {
                "title": h["title"],
                "points": h.get("points", 0),
                "comments": h.get("num_comments", 0),
                "url": f"https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id={h['objectID']}",
                "date": h.get("created_at", "")[:10],
            }
            for h in data.get("hits", [])[:max_results]
        ]
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"HN search failed for '{query}': {e}", file=sys.stderr)
        return []


def build_queries(title: str) -> list[str]:
    """Build search queries from the issue title.

    Uses the title directly plus cleaned variants.
    The title IS the idea description — no LLM needed.
    """
    import re

    # Strip common prefixes/suffixes that don't help search
    clean = title.strip()
    for prefix in ["idea:", "idea -", "[idea]"]:
        if clean.lower().startswith(prefix):
            clean = clean[len(prefix):].strip()

    queries = []
    seen = set()

    def add(q: str):
        q = q.strip()
        if q and q.lower() not in seen:
            seen.add(q.lower())
            queries.append(q)

    # Split on common separators
    parts = [clean]
    for sep in [" — ", " - ", " – ", " | "]:
        if sep in clean:
            parts = [p.strip() for p in clean.split(sep) if p.strip()]
            break

    for part in parts:
        # Strip parentheses and their content, clean punctuation
        stripped = re.sub(r"\([^)]*\)", "", part).strip()
        stripped = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", stripped).strip()
        stripped = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", stripped)
        if stripped:
            # Skip single-word names when we have a description part
            # (e.g. "Kuma" alone would match Uptime Kuma — not useful)
            if len(stripped.split()) <= 1 and len(parts) > 1:
                continue
            add(stripped)

    # Add the full cleaned title (all parts joined)
    full = " ".join(queries)
    words = full.split()
    if len(words) > 5:
        add(" ".join(words[:5]))
        add(" ".join(words[:3]))

    # Extract extra keywords from issue body if available
    if ISSUE_BODY:
        # Grab the first meaningful line from the body as an extra query
        for line in ISSUE_BODY.split("
"):
            line = line.strip().strip("#").strip("-").strip("*").strip()
            if len(line) > 10 and not line.startswith(("http", "![", "<!--")):
                body_clean = re.sub(r"[^\w\s-]", " ", line).strip()
                body_clean = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", body_clean)
                body_words = body_clean.split()
                if len(body_words) >= 3:
                    add(" ".join(body_words[:6]))
                    break

    return queries


def compute_signal(repos: list[dict], hn_posts: list[dict]) -> int:
    """Compute a 0-100 reality signal from search results."""
    score = 0

    # GitHub component (0-60)
    total_repos = len(repos)
    max_stars = max((r["stars"] for r in repos), default=0)

    if total_repos == 0:
        gh_score = 0
    elif total_repos <= 3:
        gh_score = 15
    elif total_repos <= 7:
        gh_score = 30
    else:
        gh_score = 45

    if max_stars >= 5000:
        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 20)
    elif max_stars >= 1000:
        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 15)
    elif max_stars >= 100:
        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 10)

    score += gh_score

    # HN component (0-40)
    total_hn = len(hn_posts)
    max_points = max((p["points"] for p in hn_posts), default=0)

    if total_hn == 0:
        hn_score = 0
    elif total_hn <= 2:
        hn_score = 10
    else:
        hn_score = 25

    if max_points >= 100:
        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 15)
    elif max_points >= 30:
        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 10)

    score += hn_score

    return min(100, score)


def format_comment(
    queries: list[str],
    repos: list[dict],
    hn_posts: list[dict],
    signal: int,
) -> str:
    """Format the scan results as a GitHub issue comment."""
    if signal < 30:
        verdict = "🟢 LOW — Greenfield opportunity or underserved niche"
    elif signal <= 60:
        verdict = "🟡 MODERATE — Some existing solutions, differentiation needed"
    else:
        verdict = "🔴 HIGH — Crowded space, needs strong differentiator"

    lines = [
        "## 🔍 Prior Art Scan",
        "",
        f"**Reality Signal:** {signal}/100 — {verdict}",
        f"**Queries:** {', '.join(f'`{q}`' for q in queries)}",
        "",
    ]

    # GitHub repos
    lines.append("### GitHub Repositories")
    if repos:
        lines.append("")
        lines.append("| Repo | ⭐ | Language | Description |")
        lines.append("|------|-----|----------|-------------|")
        for r in repos[:8]:
            desc = r["description"].replace("|", "\\|") if r["description"] else "—"
            lines.append(
                f"| [{r['name']}]({r['url']}) | {r['stars']:,} | {r['language']} | {desc} |"
            )
    else:
        lines.append("No relevant repositories found.")
    lines.append("")

    # HN discussions
    lines.append("### Hacker News Discussions")
    if hn_posts:
        lines.append("")
        for p in hn_posts:
            lines.append(
                f"- [{p['title']}]({p['url']}) — {p['points']} pts, "
                f"{p['comments']} comments ({p['date']})"
            )
    else:
        lines.append("No relevant discussions found.")
    lines.append("")

    lines.append("---")
    lines.append("*Auto-generated by prior-art-scan. Data informs Founder and attack agents.*")

    return "
".join(lines)


def post_comment(body: str) -> None:
    """Post a comment on the issue."""
    url = f"{GITHUB_API}/repos/{REPO}/issues/{ISSUE_NUMBER}/comments"
    resp = httpx.post(url, headers=HEADERS, json={"body": body}, timeout=15)
    resp.raise_for_status()
    print(f"Posted comment on issue #{ISSUE_NUMBER}")


def main():
    print(f"Scanning prior art for: {ISSUE_TITLE}")

    queries = build_queries(ISSUE_TITLE)
    print(f"Queries: {queries}")

    all_repos = []
    all_hn = []
    seen_repo_names = set()
    seen_hn_urls = set()

    for query in queries:
        # GitHub
        repos = search_github_repos(query)
        for r in repos:
            if r["name"] not in seen_repo_names:
                seen_repo_names.add(r["name"])
                all_repos.append(r)
        time.sleep(1)  # Rate limit

        # HN
        hn = search_hn(query)
        for h in hn:
            if h["url"] not in seen_hn_urls:
                seen_hn_urls.add(h["url"])
                all_hn.append(h)
        time.sleep(0.5)

    # Sort by relevance
    all_repos.sort(key=lambda r: r["stars"], reverse=True)
    all_hn.sort(key=lambda h: h["points"], reverse=True)

    signal = compute_signal(all_repos, all_hn)

    comment = format_comment(queries, all_repos, all_hn, signal)
    print(f"
Reality Signal: {signal}/100")
    print(f"Repos found: {len(all_repos)}, HN posts: {len(all_hn)}")

    post_comment(comment)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

  "content": "\"\"\"GitHub repository search source.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport sys\n\nimport httpx\n\nGITHUB_API = \"https://api.github.com\"\n\n\ndef search_repos(\n    query: str,\n    token: str,\n    max_results: int = 10,\n) -> list[dict]:\n    \"\"\"Search GitHub for repositories matching the query.\"\"\"\n    headers = {\n        \"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {token}\",\n        \"Accept\": \"application/vnd.github+json\",\n        \"X-GitHub-Api-Version\": \"2022-11-28\",\n    }\n    url = f\"{GITHUB_API}/search/repositories\"\n    params = {\n        \"q\": query,\n        \"sort\": \"stars\",\n        \"order\": \"desc\",\n        \"per_page\": max_results,\n    }\n    try:\n        resp = httpx.get(url, headers=headers, params=params, timeout=15)\n        resp.raise_for_status()\n        data = resp.json()\n        return [\n            {\n                \"name\": r[\"full_name\"],\n                \"stars\": r[\"stargazers_count\"],\n                \"description\": (r.get(\"description\") or \"\")[:120],\n                \"url\": r[\"html_url\"],\n                \"updated\": r[\"updated_at\"][:10],\n                \"language\": r.get(\"language\") or \"\u2014\",\n            }\n            for r in data.get(\"items\", [])[:max_results]\n        ]\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"GitHub search failed for '{query}': {e}\", file=sys.stderr)\n        return []\n"
}

Write TOOL CALL 
{
  "file_path": "/home/gem/project/src/priorart/scoring.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Reality signal computation from search results.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\n\ndef compute_signal(\n    repos: list[dict],\n    hn_posts: list[dict],\n) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Compute a 0-100 reality signal from search results.\n\n    Returns a dict with score, verdict, and breakdown.\n    \"\"\"\n    # GitHub component (0-60)\n    total_repos = len(repos)\n    max_stars = max((r[\"stars\"] for r in repos), default=0)\n\n    if total_repos == 0:\n        gh_score = 0\n    elif total_repos <= 3:\n        gh_score = 15\n    elif total_repos <= 7:\n        gh_score = 30\n    else:\n        gh_score = 45\n\n    if max_stars >= 5000:\n        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 20)\n    elif max_stars >= 1000:\n        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 15)\n    elif max_stars >= 100:\n        gh_score = min(60, gh_score + 10)\n\n    # HN component (0-40)\n    total_hn = len(hn_posts)\n    max_points = max((p[\"points\"] for p in hn_posts), default=0)\n\n    if total_hn == 0:\n        hn_score = 0\n    elif total_hn <= 2:\n        hn_score = 10\n    else:\n        hn_score = 25\n\n    if max_points >= 100:\n        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 15)\n    elif max_points >= 30:\n        hn_score = min(40, hn_score + 10)\n\n    score = min(100, gh_score + hn_score)\n\n    if score < 30:\n        verdict = \"LOW\"\n    elif score <= 60:\n        verdict = \"MODERATE\"\n    else:\n        verdict = \"HIGH\"\n\n    return {\n        \"score\": score,\n        \"verdict\": verdict,\n        \"breakdown\": {\n            \"github\": gh_score,\n            \"hn\": hn_score,\n        },\n    }\n"
}

  "content": "\"\"\"Output formatters for scan results.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport json\n\n\ndef format_json(result: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Format scan result as pretty-printed JSON.\"\"\"\n    return json.dumps(result, indent=2)\n\n\ndef format_markdown(result: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Format scan result as a GitHub-style Markdown comment.\"\"\"\n    signal = result[\"signal\"]\n    score = signal[\"score\"]\n    verdict = signal[\"verdict\"]\n    queries = result.get(\"queries\", [])\n\n    verdict_labels = {\n        \"LOW\": \"\ud83d\udfe2 LOW \u2014 Greenfield opportunity or underserved niche\",\n        \"MODERATE\": \"\ud83d\udfe1 MODERATE \u2014 Some existing solutions, differentiation needed\",\n        \"HIGH\": \"\ud83d\udd34 HIGH \u2014 Crowded space, needs strong differentiator\",\n    }\n    verdict_str = verdict_labels.get(verdict, verdict)\n\n    lines = [\n        \"## \ud83d\udd0d Prior Art Scan\",\n        \"\",\n        f\"**Reality Signal:** {score}/100 \u2014 {verdict_str}\",\n        f\"**Queries:** {', '.join(f'`{q}`' for q in queries)}\",\n        \"\",\n    ]\n\n    # GitHub repos\n    repos = next(\n        (s[\"results\"] for s in result.get(\"sources\", []) if s[\"type\"] == \"github\"),\n        [],\n    )\n    lines.append(\"### GitHub Repositories\")\n    if repos:\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        lines.append(\"| Repo | \u2b50 | Language | Description |\")\n        lines.append(\"|------|-----|----------|-------------|\")\n        for r in repos[:8]:\n            desc = (r.get(\"description\") or \"\u2014\").replace(\"|\", \"\\\\|\")\n            lines.append(\n                f\"| [{r['name']}]({r['url']}) | {r['stars']:,} | {r['language']} | {desc} |\"\n            )\n    else:\n        lines.append(\"No relevant repositories found.\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # HN discussions\n    hn_posts = next(\n        (s[\"results\"] for s in result.get(\"sources\", []) if s[\"type\"] == \"hn\"),\n        [],\n    )\n    lines.append(\"### Hacker News Discussions\")\n    if hn_posts:\n        lines.append(\"\")\n        for p in hn_posts:\n            lines.append(\n                f\"- [{p['title']}]({p['url']}) \u2014 {p['points']} pts, \"\n                f\"{p['comments']} comments ({p['date']})\"\n            )\n    else:\n        lines.append(\"No relevant discussions found.\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    lines.append(\"---\")\n    lines.append(\n        \"*Auto-generated by priorart. Data informs Founder and attack agents.*\"\n    )\n\n    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n\ndef format_table(result: dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Format scan result as plain-text tables.\"\"\"\n    signal = result[\"signal\"]\n    score = signal[\"score\"]\n    verdict = signal[\"verdict\"]\n    queries = result.get(\"queries\", [])\n\n    lines = [\n        \"Prior Art Scan\",\n        \"=\" * 60,\n        f\"Reality Signal: {score}/100  ({verdict})\",\n        f\"Queries: {', '.join(queries)}\",\n        \"\",\n    ]\n\n    # GitHub repos\n    repos = next(\n        (s[\"results\"] for s in result.get(\"sources\", []) if s[\"type\"] == \"github\"),\n        [],\n    )\n    lines.append(\"GitHub Repositories\")\n    lines.append(\"-\" * 60)\n    if repos:\n        col_widths = {\"name\": 35, \"stars\": 8, \"language\": 12, \"description\": 40}\n        header = (\n            f\"{'Repo':<{col_widths['name']}} \"\n            f\"{'Stars':>{col_widths['stars']}} \"\n            f\"{'Language':<{col_widths['language']}} \"\n            f\"Description\"\n        )\n        lines.append(header)\n        lines.append(\"-\" * 60)\n        for r in repos[:8]:\n            name = r[\"name\"][: col_widths[\"name\"]]\n            desc = (r.get(\"description\") or \"\u2014\")[: col_widths[\"description\"]]\n            lang = (r.get(\"language\") or \"\u2014\")[: col_widths[\"language\"]]\n            lines.append(\n                f\"{name:<{col_widths['name']}} \"\n                f\"{r['stars']:>{col_widths['stars']},} \"\n                f\"{lang:<{col_widths['language']}} \"\n                f\"{desc}\"\n            )\n    else:\n        lines.append(\"No relevant repositories found.\")\n    lines.append(\"\")\n\n    # HN discussions\n    hn_posts = next(\n        (s[\"results\"] for s in result.get(\"sources\", []) if s[\"type\"] == \"hn\"),\n        [],\n    )\n    lines.append(\"Hacker News Discussions\")\n    lines.append(\"-\" * 60)\n    if hn_posts:\n        for p in hn_posts:\n            title = p[\"title\"][:55]\n            lines.append(f\"  {title}\")\n            lines.append(\n                f\"    {p['points']} pts, {p['comments']} comments  {p['date']}\"\n            )\n            lines.append(f\"    {p['url']}\")\n    else:\n        lines.append(\"No relevant discussions found.\")\n\n    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n"

  "content": "\"\"\"Orchestrator \u2014 builds queries, runs sources, computes signal.\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nimport time\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\n\nfrom priorart import __version__\nfrom priorart.scoring import compute_signal\nfrom priorart.sources.github import search_repos\nfrom priorart.sources.hn import search_discussions\n\n\ndef build_queries(title: str, body: str = \"\") -> list[str]:\n    \"\"\"Build search queries from the idea title (and optional body).\n\n    Uses the title directly plus cleaned variants.\n    The title IS the idea description \u2014 no LLM needed.\n    \"\"\"\n    clean = title.strip()\n    for prefix in [\"idea:\", \"idea -\", \"[idea]\"]:\n        if clean.lower().startswith(prefix):\n            clean = clean[len(prefix) :].strip()\n\n    queries: list[str] = []\n    seen: set[str] = set()\n\n    def add(q: str) -> None:\n        q = q.strip()\n        if q and q.lower() not in seen:\n            seen.add(q.lower())\n            queries.append(q)\n\n    # Split on common separators\n    parts = [clean]\n    for sep in [\" \u2014 \", \" - \", \" \u2013 \", \" | \"]:\n        if sep in clean:\n            parts = [p.strip() for p in clean.split(sep) if p.strip()]\n            break\n\n    for part in parts:\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"\\([^)]*\\)\", \"\", part).strip()\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"[^\\w\\s-]\", \" \", stripped).strip()\n        stripped = re.sub(r\"\\s+\", \" \", stripped)\n        if stripped:\n            if len(stripped.split()) <= 1 and len(parts) > 1:\n                continue\n            add(stripped)\n\n    full = \" \".join(queries)\n    words = full.split()\n    if len(words) > 5:\n        add(\" \".join(words[:5]))\n        add(\" \".join(words[:3]))\n\n    if body:\n        for line in body.split(\"\\n\"):\n            line = line.strip().strip(\"#\").strip(\"-\").strip(\"*\").strip()\n            if len(line) > 10 and not line.startswith((\"http\", \"![\", \"<!--\")):\n                body_clean = re.sub(r\"[^\\w\\s-]\", \" \", line).strip()\n                body_clean = re.sub(r\"\\s+\", \" \", body_clean)\n                body_words = body_clean.split()\n                if len(body_words) >= 3:\n                    add(\" \".join(body_words[:6]))\n                    break\n\n    return queries\n\n\ndef scan(\n    idea: str,\n    github_token: str | None = None,\n    sources: list[str] | None = None,\n    body: str = \"\",\n) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Run a full prior-art scan and return structured results.\n\n    Args:\n        idea: The idea description to scan.\n        github_token: GitHub personal access token (required for GitHub source).\n        sources: List of source names to query. Defaults to [\"github\", \"hn\"].\n        body: Optional body text for additional query extraction.\n\n    Returns:\n        Structured dict: {query, queries, sources, signal, meta}\n    \"\"\"\n    if sources is None:\n        sources = [\"github\", \"hn\"]\n\n    queries = build_queries(idea, body)\n\n    all_repos: list[dict] = []\n    all_hn: list[dict] = []\n    seen_repo_names: set[str] = set()\n    seen_hn_urls: set[str] = set()\n\n    for query in queries:\n        if \"github\" in sources and github_token:\n            repos = search_repos(query, github_token)\n            for r in repos:\n                if r[\"name\"] not in seen_repo_names:\n                    seen_repo_names.add(r[\"name\"])\n                    all_repos.append(r)\n            time.sleep(1)\n\n        if \"hn\" in sources:\n            hn = search_discussions(query)\n            for h in hn:\n                if h[\"url\"] not in seen_hn_urls:\n                    seen_hn_urls.add(h[\"url\"])\n                    all_hn.append(h)\n            time.sleep(0.5)\n\n    all_repos.sort(key=lambda r: r[\"stars\"], reverse=True)\n    all_hn.sort(key=lambda h: h[\"points\"], reverse=True)\n\n    signal = compute_signal(all_repos, all_hn)\n\n    source_results = []\n    if \"github\" in sources:\n        source_results.append({\"type\": \"github\", \"results\": all_repos})\n    if \"hn\" in sources:\n        source_results.append({\"type\": \"hn\", \"results\": all_hn})\n\n    return {\n        \"query\": idea,\n        \"queries\": queries,\n        \"sources\": source_results,\n        \"signal\": signal,\n        \"meta\": {\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n            \"version\": __version__,\n        },\n    }\n"
}

Choose from: github, hn\",\n                err=True,\n            )\n            raise typer.Exit(code=1)\n\n    if \"github\" in source_list and not github_token:\n        typer.echo(\n            \"Warning: GitHub source requested but no GITHUB_TOKEN found. \"\n            \"Skipping GitHub search.\",\n            err=True,\n        )\n\n    result = scan(idea, github_token=github_token, sources=source_list)\n\n    if fmt == \"json\":\n        typer.echo(format_json(result))\n    elif fmt == \"markdown\":\n        typer.echo(format_markdown(result))\n    else:\n        typer.echo(format_table(result))\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    app()\n"

  "content": "\"\"\"Tests for scanner module \u2014 query building.\"\"\"\n\nimport pytest\n\nfrom priorart.scanner import build_queries\n\n\nclass TestBuildQueries:\n    def test_simple_idea(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"AI personal finance tracker\")\n        assert len(queries) >= 1\n        assert \"AI personal finance tracker\" in queries\n\n    def test_strips_idea_prefix(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"idea: AI personal finance tracker\")\n        for q in queries:\n            assert not q.lower().startswith(\"idea:\")\n\n    def test_strips_idea_bracket_prefix(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"[idea] AI personal finance tracker\")\n        for q in queries:\n            assert not q.lower().startswith(\"[idea]\")\n\n    def test_splits_on_dash_separator(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"Kuma \u2014 Self-hosted uptime monitor\")\n        # Should produce multi-word queries, not just \"Kuma\"\n        assert any(len(q.split()) > 1 for q in queries)\n\n    def test_splits_on_em_dash(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"FinTrack \u2014 AI finance tracker\")\n        assert any(\"AI finance tracker\" in q or \"finance tracker\" in q for q in queries)\n\n    def test_long_title_adds_shortened_variants(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"AI-powered personal finance tracking application for mobile\")\n        # Should add 5-word and 3-word variants\n        assert len(queries) >= 2\n\n    def test_no_duplicate_queries(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"AI personal finance tracker\")\n        lower = [q.lower() for q in queries]\n        assert len(lower) == len(set(lower))\n\n    def test_body_adds_extra_query(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\n            \"Finance app\",\n            body=\"Smart budgeting with machine learning insights\",\n        )\n        assert any(\"Smart budgeting\" in q or \"budgeting\" in q for q in queries)\n\n    def test_body_ignores_http_lines(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\n            \"Finance app\",\n            body=\"https://example.com/something\\nSmart budgeting tool\",\n        )\n        # URL line should be skipped\n        for q in queries:\n            assert \"https://\" not in q\n\n    def test_returns_list_of_strings(self):\n        queries = build_queries(\"test idea\")\n        assert isinstance(queries, list)\n        assert all(isinstance(q, str) for q in queries)\n\n    def test_empty_title_edge_case(self):\n        # Should not raise, returns whatever makes sense\n        queries = build_queries(\"   \")\n        assert isinstance(queries, list)\n"

  "content": "# priorart\n\nPrior art scanner for ideas. Searches GitHub repositories and Hacker News discussions to assess how crowded a space is, then produces a **Reality Signal** score (0\u2013100).\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\npip install priorart\n```\n\nOr with `uv`:\n\n```bash\nuv add priorart\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n# Basic scan (table output)\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker'\n\n# JSON output\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format json\n\n# Markdown output (same format as GitHub Action comment)\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format markdown\n\n# Limit to specific sources\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --sources hn\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --sources github,hn\n\n# With explicit GitHub token\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --github-token ghp_...\n```\n\nThe `GITHUB_TOKEN` environment variable is used automatically if set:\n\n```bash\nexport GITHUB_TOKEN=ghp_...\npriorart scan 'AI personal finance tracker' --format json\n```\n\n## Output formats\n\n### JSON (`--format json`)\n\n```json\n{\n  \"query\": \"AI personal finance tracker\",\n  \"queries\": [\"AI personal finance tracker\", \"AI personal finance\"],\n  \"sources\": [\n    {\n      \"type\": \"github\",\n      \"results\": [\n        {\n          \"name\": \"org/repo\",\n          \"stars\": 1234,\n          \"description\": \"...\",\n          \"url\": \"https://github.com/org/repo\",\n          \"updated\": \"2024-01-01\",\n          \"language\": \"Python\"\n        }\n      ]\n    },\n    {\n      \"type\": \"hn\",\n      \"results\": [\n        {\n          \"title\": \"...\",\n          \"points\": 42,\n          \"comments\": 17,\n          \"url\": \"https://news.ycombinator.com/item?id=...\",\n          \"date\": \"2024-03-01\"\n        }\n      ]\n    }\n  ],\n  \"signal\": {\n    \"score\": 45,\n    \"verdict\": \"MODERATE\",\n    \"breakdown\": {\n      \"github\": 30,\n      \"hn\": 15\n    }\n  },\n  \"meta\": {\n    \"timestamp\": \"2026-03-07T00:00:00+00:00\",\n    \"version\": \"0.1.0\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Markdown (`--format markdown`)\n\nProduces the same Markdown comment format used by the `prior-art-scan` GitHub Action.\n\n### Table (`--format table`)\n\nPlain-text table for terminal output (default).\n\n## Reality Signal\n\nThe Reality Signal (0\u2013100) reflects how crowded the solution space is:\n\n| Score | Verdict | Meaning |\n|-------|---------|---------|\n| 0\u201329 | \ud83d\udfe2 LOW | Greenfield opportunity or underserved niche |\n| 30\u201360 | \ud83d\udfe1 MODERATE | Some existing solutions, differentiation needed |\n| 61\u2013100 | \ud83d\udd34 HIGH | Crowded space, needs strong differentiator |\n\nThe score is composed of:\n- **GitHub component (0\u201360):** number of repos found + max star count\n- **HN component (0\u201340):** number of discussions found + max point count\n\n## Development\n\n```bash\n# Install with dev dependencies\npip install -e \".[dev]\"\n\n# Run tests\npytest\n\n# Lint\nruff check src tests\n```\n\n## Package structure\n\n```\nsrc/priorart/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 __init__.py       # version\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 scanner.py        # orchestrator + query builder\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 scoring.py        # reality signal computation\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 formatters.py     # JSON, markdown, table output\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 cli.py            # typer CLI entry point\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 sources/\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 __init__.py\n    \u251c\u2500\u2500 github.py     # GitHub repository search\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 hn.py         # Hacker News search (Algolia API)\n```\n"

**PR:** https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/priorart/pull/1
**Branch:** `feature/frg-191-scaffold-package-extract-core-cli-json-output`

### What was built

Scaffolded the `priorart` Python package from scratch by extracting and restructuring all logic from `prior-art-scan.py`:

**Package structure (`src/priorart/`):**
- `scanner.py` — orchestrator + `build_queries()` (all original query logic preserved)
- `sources/github.py` — GitHub repo search (extracted from original)
- `sources/hn.py` — HN search via Algolia (extracted from original)
- `scoring.py` — reality signal computation (0–100, with breakdown)
- `formatters.py` — JSON, markdown (same format as GitHub Action comment), and table
- `cli.py` — `priorart scan '<idea>' --format json|markdown|table --sources github,hn`

**Config/infra:**
- `pyproject.toml` with hatchling build backend (matches RepoCrunch pattern), `typer` + `httpx` deps
- `README.md` with usage examples, output format docs, and package structure
- `.gitignore`

**Tests (36 passing):**
- `tests/test_scoring.py` — signal computation, verdict thresholds, score cap
- `tests/test_formatters.py` — JSON validity, markdown structure, table output
- `tests/test_scanner.py` — query building, prefix stripping, separator splitting, body extraction

### Key decisions

- **`requires-python = \">=3.11\"`** — matches RepoCrunch pattern; Python 3.10 (system default) not supported
- **`queries` added to JSON output** — the spec shows `{query, sources, signal, meta}` but storing the expanded query list in the output is useful for debugging and transparency; `query` (original idea) is still the top-level key
- **GitHub token** — read from `GITHUB_TOKEN` env var or `--github-token` flag; emits a warning and skips GitHub source if missing (rather than crashing)
- **Markdown formatter** — exactly matches the original `format_comment()` output format, including the verdict emoji labels
